THE KING OF JERKS
4/1/2012
Helenaelise
Meet Ran! The prettiest cosplayer in the campus! and Meet Rigid! the imposing dictator president of the Student Council. Paano kung ang cosplayer na ito at ang taong bato ay mag clash? since parehong ayaw magpatalo...ayaw masabihang mali. Nagkaroon sila ng dare na sadyang kakaiba, sino kaya ang unang susuko?

O di sige siya na henyo! =_= prodigy daw ang tawag sa kanya ng mga scientist, yung mga abnormal na tao na...na...wait tignan natin meaning ng prodigy sa dictionary <scan...> <scan////>
ayun! prodigy! ay teka mali pedigree anu siya aso? hmm pede na din! eyun! eto eto na talaga! copy pasted pa yan! [prod-i-jee] –noun, plural -gies. 1. a person, especially a child or young person, havingextraordinary talent or ability: a musical prodigy. 2. a marvelous example (usually followed by of ). 3. something wonderful or marvelous; a wonder. 4. something abnormal or monstrous. 5. Archaic . something extraordinary regarded as of propheticsignificance. prod·i·gy Sa lahat ng depinisyon sa kanya dito ay dun lang ako sa number four nag-aagree! o di sige siya na prodigy! abnormal and monstrous! wahehehehehe! pero biglang natigil yung pagtawa ko ng makita ko siya, oo na sige na inaamin ko na ang gwapo nga niya, kumag peste! di sige siya na perfect. "Hindi ko nagustuhan yung ginawa mo kanina, no one has ever treated me as boorishly as you did today" he said in a calm demeanor, but the fire in his eyes was scorching. Nakakatakot nga ito! Teka lang! ano'ng karapatan niyang iintimidate ako! ako si Ran Figueroa! hindi mo ako maiintimidate! nek nek mo! "Ano ngayon?" balik ko sa kanya, mukhang hindi naman ito nasindak sa sinabi ko, bagkus (nosebleed!) ngumiti pa ito, ay mali! hindi pala ngiti, ngisi pala! ngumisi ito, yung tipong matatakot ka para sa buhay mo, pero ayoko! ayoko maintimidate! hindeeeee!!!! tinititgan ko din siya ayoko magback down. "Your attitude is boorish, and you dress in a deviant fashion, I don't know if you're just plain stubborn, or you're fishing for attention. One thing is for sure though, as long as I'm the president in this school I won't let anyone slip and break the rules." sabi nito, contained anger mirrored in his eyes, pero aba~! sumosobra na ito ah! Fishing for attention? ako! hangkapal ng mukha! kumalma ka Ran, kalma lang kundi hahambalusin ko na itong gagong ito, oo alam ko masama magmura pero mas masama kung hinahayaang gumala gala sa mundong ibabaw ang katulad ng herodes na ito. Antipatiko, balasubas, halimaw, mamaw, walanghiya at---- "No wonder wala kang boyfriend, kasi puro pagpapaganda lang ang alam mo." sabi pa nito in a disgusted tone bago ako binitawan, sa gulat ko gumalaw ang sarili kong mga kamay at sinampal siya, napabaling sa kabilang direction ang mukha nito, but I saw him smirk nonetheless. "Ang kapal din ng mukha---" my words halted as may naglarong idea sa isip ko, ibinaba ko yung kamay kong sumampal sa kanya sa ere, at nginitian siya. "Fine, I don't have anything to prove to you Rigid Razor Montez, but now that you've provoked me, I suggest you be ready, one day you'll eat your words and I swear to my grandmere's grave, you'll be crawling on your knees in no time, I will make your life a living scenario in hell." ngiti ko sa kanya saka umalis, with my poise ang everything intact. I refuse to let him rip me out of my pride, magdurusa ka! Rigid Razor Montez! I swear! sabi ko sarili ko at naglakad palayo.
Rigid's POV Napangiti ako sukat sa tinuran ng babae, should I be afraid now? I released a lop-sided grin to myself, at times yun na yata ang worst na babaeng nakita ko sa tanang buhay ko. Hindi maintindihan, mas madali pa ang quantum physics intindihin kesa sa kanya, I must admit, I went out of line sa mga nasabi ko sa kanya, but hell will freeze over before I take back my words. "Ms. Figueroa!" tawag ko sa papalayong babae, nakita kong tumigil ito sa paglalakad, ngunit hindi tumingin sa akin. "Please do so. And I'll gladly return the favor" sabi ko saka ko siya tinalikuran, it's not that I'm being an ungentleman, pero ang mga ugaling ganoon, hindi dapat tinotolerate. But I must admit, for a moment there nawalan ako ng tolerance makipagdeal sa kanya. Naglakad na ako pabalik sa student council room. Napangiti ako to see the orderliness in the school, OC na kung OC pero mas maganda pag maayos. People call me as dictator, that I rule with steel hands, but my point is, it's a lot better than to have a school which can be compared to slums. Lahat ng estudyanteng malagpasan ko I see their eyes glimmer with admiration, it's not like I am conceited or soimething but...haay...being a prodigy is a tough job. Eversince I was a kid, pinagaaralan na ako ng mga scientist, I have this uncanny ability to understand everything in just a flash, I just have to attenc formal schooling for formalities sake but I already handle a share of our family businesses, madali akong matuto sa isang bagay ngunit madali din ako magsawa, I don't find anything thrilling in this world anymore, lahat simple, I might sound conceited and boastful now pero I'm really bored with this life. Lahat nalang ang tingin sa akin kakaiba, pati tuloy si Lena, my little sister thinks that she is too ordinary. She can't see how wonderful she is just because she always gets compared with me. Napabuntong hininga nalang ako. As I looked at the paperworks in front of me. Siguro ang mga ito nag-o-orgy sa gabi ano? dumadami kinabukasan eh. Napasimangot nalang ako ng magring ang cellphone ko, it was Rina again. sigh...ito pa ang isang ayaw ko sa srili ko, lagi nalang ako nabeblame na cassanova, just because I end up a relationship too quickly, eh ano ba ang magagawa ko? eh sa madali nga ako magsawa eh, redundant nalang naman kasi ang nangyayari. Kesa naman I keep the girl kahit it's quite evident na hindi na ako masaya. That's selfish yes but it's even worse kung magpanggap akong masaya pa. A relationship is good till it lasts anyway.
Inayos ko ang paperworks sa table ko. At nagsimula na, may klase pa kasi ako mamaya. I was halfway through my paperworks when I remembered that girl again, hindi lang miminsan siyang sumingit sa train of thoughts ko for the past few minutes, natawa nalang ako, I rested back on my chair at nag abot ng isang malinis na bond paper, and before I knew it I was drawing her face. She had a very beautiful face, sayang kung hindi sana siya isang napakalaking sakit ng ulo okay sana siya....what the--??? Hinding hindi ako papatol sa isang babaeng ganoon, now where did that come from? I neatly folded the paper and looked at it again and then dropped it to the shreder, she's gonna make a living scenario of hell in my life huh? well I'd like to see her try. That is if...I don't make her life hell first, now that I found something to ease up my boredom. Just then tumayo ako, nakita ko ang matabang lalaki kanina na itinaboy ng babaeng amazona. Teka, umiiyak ba ito? "Ran...huhuhu...bakit? bakit ba hindi mo ako magustuhan?" sabi nito, I didn't mean to eavesdrop pero, parang gusto ko matawa, a guy? shedding tears for a girl? I'm sorry but that's just lame. Aalis na sana ako pero narinig ko ang mga huling sinabi nito. "Magiging akin ka today Ran, by hook or by crook" sabi nito at lumayo. Hindi ko alam kung ano ang nangyari, but my heart skipped a beat at pinagpawisan ako bigla, this is not an arrhythmia is it? do I need to have an ECG exam? no...I'll take one later, right now I need to save that girl, kahit sakit pa siya ng ulo. Babae pa din siya, at estudyante pa din siya ng paaralang ito. With that thought I dashed off to follow that guy. __to be continued.

Sabi nga ng isang napakatalinong babae na crush ko (yung author hahaha! ang feelingera ko eh noh? -author) Romantic love feelings commence in the region of the lower brain that is known as the hypothalamus. The hypothalamus is composed of a dense cluster of nerves which controls hundreds of bodily functions and impacts in a large host of ways the entire nervous system. Whenever a person subjectively perceives another human being as romantically appealing a portion of the hypothalamus transmits a message by way of various chemicals to the pituitary gland. And in turn the pituitary releases a host of its own hormones which rapidly suffuse the entire bloodstream. The sex glands respond to these hormones by rapidly releasing into the bloodstream their own
hormones which have the effect, even among preadolescent children, of creating a more rapid heartbeat and a feeling of lightness in the head. Simultaneously the nerve pathways in and around the hypothalamus produce chemicals that induce-provided that these chemicals continued to be produced over a long period of time-what people refer to as "falling in love". -Helenaelise (Random thoughts from a Defective Hypothalamus) see? she explained the science of love and it is all just a product of the mind, it is explainable and hence it is controllable. Napangiti ako ng makita ko doon ang panyo niyang ninakaw ko sa US noon, ng gawin namin si Kikuri...then ultrasound pictures of Kikuri...her first smile...her first leaf na pinulot, pati ang unang langgam na pinatay niya. Vast collection of KIkuri's daily pictures...then it was then again ng bumalik si Rigid sa buhay naming magina. And we became a complete family...
Napaluha ako buti nalang maagap si Rain at pinunasan ang luha ko para hindi magsmudge. "Haay naku ikakasal nalang kayo iiyak ka pa?" sabi nito sa akin ngumiti lang ako sa kanya. It's time to start a new scrap book...dahil magsisimula na ang mga buhay naming magkakasama. "Thanks Rain" I whispered. Third Person's POV "Kuya ano ka ba para kang matatae na ewan jan! umayos ka nga!" sabi ni Lena sa kapatid, Rigid was fussing all over hindi sure kung ano'ng gagawin. "Bakit wala pa siya?" he said, "Baka nakidnap na siya o kaya...o kaya"
"My goodness Kuya! nasa kabilang hotel lang sila umayos ka nga! Si Aston ang maghahatid sa kanya" sabi ni Lena para kalmahin ang kapatid. "Nako Lena, malalagot sa akin yang fiancee mo kapag---" hindi na naituloy ni Rigid ang sasabihin niya ng makita nila ang isang puting limousine sa beach. Then Reino's band began to play their thing, kaduet nito si Rain. (A/N: le song over zere --------------------------------------> ) Rigid's eyes dilated as Ran descended from the car. His life...his goddess...the only queen of his heart...then an overwhelming sensation swelled in his heart... Ang babaeng nagbigay ng buhay sa mundo niya. He smiled, he couldn't believe na matutupad na din sa wakas ang kanilang mga pangarap. Beside her was their little girl trailing along as the little bride. Halos lumuwa ang mga mata ni Ran sa pagkakita sa paligid...ang..ang kanilang traditional wedding...nagmistulang isang anime convention! their guests were..were wearing anime costumes! lahat! even Rigid's parents!
Lena was sailor moon and and...nilingon ko si Aston na naka-tuxedo mask na! Kumakanta si Rain as Haruhi Suzumiya at si Reino si Kyon! Even Kyle was there and...and various others! may mecha..may schoolgirl! at..at... Nagulat ito ng lumapit sa kanya ang ama ni Rigid nakacosplay din ito siya ang maghahatid sa kanya sa altar,...sa kanyang si Lelouch... Umuulan ng petals sa paligid nalia pero mistulang wala itong ibang nakikita kundi si Rigid laman...he was smiling at her lalo na ng magsimula na ang wedding march. Nakarating sila sa harap ni Rigid ng ipasa ng ama ni Rigid si Ran sa binata. "Take care you two.." sabi ng ama ni Rigid sa kanila, Ran smiled at him as he returned his smile. (A/N: picture -------------------------------------------->) He took her hand in his arm as they strode towards the altar. Bearing their vows in their hearts.
Ng matapos magsalita ang pari, it was time for their vows. Humarap si Rigid dito. "I won't say a normal vow, because the moment you entered my life my monotonous and boring existence...mula ng makita ko ang naghuhumindig na green mong buhok ay you already made your mark on me...hindi ko akalaing ang mark na iyon ang sasakop sa puso ko. When you left me, I felt like the world crashed before me and when I found you and Kikuri again...nalaman kong mahal ako ng Diyos...dahil binalik ka niya sa akin" he said as he held her face in his hands pinunasan ni Ran ang luha ng lalaking minamahal Then it was her turn... "Rigid...noong una, asar talaga ako sa iyo...lagi mo nalang akong sinisita, then as fast as a bullet, no..maybe even faster I fell for you...hard! lalo na at ikaw lang ang tanging taong dumating sa buhay ko who taught me how to love...ng masaktan ka ng dahil sa akin I nerly died kaya ko lumayo sa iyo, then we saw each other again...and then there was Kikuri...the greatest gift in our lives...and now, even after all these years...here we are...inside each other's arms..." Then after saying their vows and exchanging their rings. "I now pronounce you as man and wife. You may now kiss the bride" the priest said. And without preamble he lifted her veil as he kissed her with the promise of eternity.
"I love you my queen" he whispered "I love you more...my King of Jerks" she said as she smiled "Mommy't Daddy ko yaaaaan!!!!" Kikuri shouted as they all rejoiced. Epilogue Ibinaba ni Rigid si Ran sa kanyang mga bisig at siniil ito ng halik sa labi. Bukas ay pupunta sila ng Europe silang magpapamilya...pero ngayon...silang dalawa lang muna... "Mrs. Ran Figueroa-Montez" he said as he kissed her. Ran smiled, napakagandang pakinggan, as they were kissing each other, naupo sila sa kama... Rigid held her face as he reached the zipper of her wedding gown. When the door burst open!
O________O Sabay pa silang napalingon sa pintuan and Kikuri was there along with Lena! "Err...she wanted to see you daw eh" sabi ni Lena "Mommy! Daddy! Yey!!! One happy family na tayo!!!" sigaw nito "I'll sleep beside the two of you!!!" masayang sabi nito, nanlaki ang mga mata ni Rigid sa narinig, tumawa lang ang kanyang asawa. "Baby you can't..." he said "Why daddy?" she said inoccently "May gagawin kami ng mommy mo eh" he said as he grinned, nanlaki ang mga mata ni Ran sa sinabi ni Rigid...he can't possibly be serious!
Tumawa lang si Lena sa background. "Ano po iyon daddy?" she said innocently "Baby brother mo" he said as Ran laughed and kissed their daughter in the cheek, namilog ang mga mata ni Kikuri saka ngumiti ng maluwag at nagtatatalon sa kama. "Yey!!! magkaka baby-brother na ako! Goodluck mommy! Goodluck daddy! His name will be Poropompom!" nagtatatalon na sabi niya saka humalik sa mga magulang. At tumakbo kay Lena as they shut the door. Tumayo si Rigid at nilock ang pinto. Hindi pa nakuntento ay tinulak pa nito ang aparador sa pinto, tumawa lang ng malakas si Ran. "Now where were we?" he said at lumapit sa asawa "Kay Poropompom?" natatawang sabi ni Ran sa asawa. Ngumiwi lang si Rigid as he started loosing his tie.
"nah...I prefer Rigid Jr." he said as he joined his wife to bed at sinimulan na nilang gawin si Rigid Jr. - F I N - ayoon finally I was able to finish this. Maraming salamat po sa mga sumuporta lalo na noong paumpisa palang ito! sana po ay patuloy niyo pong suportahan ang iba ko pa ponbg kwento dahil mahilig mag cross over ang mga characters ko hehehe XD ayun lang po!
